But toggleActive validates the raw input first and throws an error if it doesn't match—it's stricter and doesn't allow shorthand names like 'imgur'. The test for toggleActive expects both '\\t\\nnodebb-plugin' and 'not aplugin' to fail validation, which they do since neither matches the required pattern.\n\nThe CLI's approach is more flexible: it attempts to normalize shorthand inputs by adding the prefix, then validates the result. So 'imgur' becomes 'nodebb-plugin-imgur' and gets validated. This means the CLI fixes ensure that even after prefix addition, the final name still passes validation.\n\nTesting the flow with problematic inputs shows the validation catches them appropriately—malformed names like '\\t\\nnodebb-plugin' become invalid after prefixing, and 'notaplugin' passes the pattern check but would fail at the installation check later.\n\nThe core issue is that `toggleActive()` doesn't add prefixes, so it rejects unprefixed names directly.
